kimi-k2.6
Stop — Don't Run the Original Schema Again. Run the UPGRADE Only.
Your tables (customers, orders, deliveries, etc.) were created on Day 1. That's why you're getting "relation already exists" — you're trying to recreate what already exists.

You only need the UPGRADE script — the one that adds new columns and the pricing matrix on top of your existing tables.

Step 1: Open Supabase SQL Editor
Go to: https://supabase.com/dashboard/project/ukrztdeqzbbroowcphwk/sql/new

Step 2: Paste ONLY This Upgrade Script
This assumes your 6 original tables already exist. It only adds what's new.

SQL
-- ============================================================
-- UPGRADE SCRIPT ONLY — Tables already exist from Day 1
-- ============================================================

-- 1. Cleanup any conflicting AI-generated views
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS subscription_overview CASCADE;
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS subscription_offers CASCADE;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS subscription_offers CASCADE;

DO $$
DECLARE
    v RECORD;
BEGIN
    FOR v IN SELECT viewname FROM pg_views WHERE schemaname = 'public' AND viewname LIKE 'subscription%' LOOP
        EXECUTE 'DROP VIEW IF EXISTS public.' || quote_ident(v.viewname) || ' CASCADE';
    END LOOP;
END $$;

-- 2. Add new columns safely (won't break existing data)
ALTER TABLE orders ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS meal_session TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'lunch' 
  CHECK (meal_session IN ('lunch', 'dinner', 'both'));

ALTER TABLE deliveries ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS credits_burn INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1 CHECK (credits_burn > 0);

ALTER TABLE plans ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS duration_days INTEGER;
ALTER TABLE plans ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS plan_type TEXT CHECK (plan_type IN ('regular', 'student', 'addon'));
ALTER TABLE plans ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS bonus_credits INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0;

ALTER TABLE orders ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS delivery_charges NUMERIC(10,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 CHECK (delivery_charges >= 0);

-- 3. Create pricing matrix (new table)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS plan_menu_pricing (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  plan_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES plans(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  menu_item_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES menu_items(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  price NUMERIC(10,2) NOT NULL CHECK (price >= 0),
  active BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT true,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  UNIQUE (plan_id, menu_item_id)
);

ALTER TABLE plan_menu_pricing ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
DROP POLICY IF EXISTS "allow_all_plan_menu_pricing" ON plan_menu_pricing;
CREATE POLICY "allow_all_plan_menu_pricing" ON plan_menu_pricing FOR ALL USING (true) WITH CHECK (true);

-- 4. Replace trigger function with upgraded version
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION handle_delivery_status_change()
RETURNS TRIGGER
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_order_type    TEXT;
  v_plan_credits  INTEGER;
  v_credits_used  INTEGER;
  v_latest_date   DATE;
  v_meal_session  TEXT;
  v_credits_burn  INTEGER;
BEGIN
  IF TG_OP = 'UPDATE' AND OLD.status = NEW.status THEN
    RETURN NEW;
  END IF;

  SELECT order_type, plan_credits, credits_used, meal_session
    INTO v_order_type, v_plan_credits, v_credits_used, v_meal_session
    FROM orders WHERE id = NEW.order_id;
  
  v_credits_burn := CASE WHEN v_meal_session = 'both' THEN 2 ELSE 1 END;

  IF NEW.status = 'delivered' AND OLD.status != 'delivered' THEN
    UPDATE orders
       SET credits_used = LEAST(credits_used + v_credits_burn, plan_credits)
     WHERE id = NEW.order_id;
  END IF;

  IF NEW.status = 'missed' AND OLD.status != 'missed' THEN
    IF v_order_type = 'subscription' THEN
      SELECT credits_used INTO v_credits_used FROM orders WHERE id = NEW.order_id;
      IF v_credits_used < v_plan_credits THEN
        SELECT MAX(scheduled_date) INTO v_latest_date FROM deliveries WHERE order_id = NEW.order_id;
        INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
          VALUES (NEW.order_id, v_latest_date + INTERVAL '1 day', 'pending', v_credits_burn)
          ON CONFLICT (order_id, scheduled_date) DO NOTHING;
      END IF;
    END IF;
  END IF;

  RETURN NEW;
END;
$$;

-- 5. Replace order creation function with upgraded version
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION create_order_with_deliveries(
  p_customer_id    UUID,
  p_menu_item_id   UUID,
  p_order_type     TEXT,
  p_plan_id        UUID,
  p_plan_credits   INTEGER,
  p_total_amount   NUMERIC,
  p_payment_status TEXT,
  p_payment_mode   TEXT,
  p_notes          TEXT,
  p_start_date     DATE,
  p_meal_session   TEXT DEFAULT 'lunch',
  p_delivery_charges NUMERIC DEFAULT 0
)
RETURNS UUID
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_order_id    UUID;
  v_menu_active BOOLEAN;
  v_credits_per_day INTEGER;
  v_num_days    INTEGER;
  v_remainder   INTEGER;
  v_i           INTEGER;
BEGIN
  SELECT active INTO v_menu_active FROM menu_items WHERE id = p_menu_item_id;
  IF v_menu_active IS NULL THEN RAISE EXCEPTION 'Menu item not found';
  ELSIF v_menu_active = false THEN RAISE EXCEPTION 'This menu item is no longer active';
  END IF;

  IF p_order_type = 'subscription' AND (p_plan_id IS NULL OR p_plan_credits IS NULL) THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Subscription orders require a plan';
  END IF;
  IF p_start_date IS NULL THEN RAISE EXCEPTION 'A delivery start date is required'; END IF;

  v_credits_per_day := CASE WHEN p_meal_session = 'both' THEN 2 ELSE 1 END;

  INSERT INTO orders (
    customer_id, menu_item_id, order_type, plan_id, plan_credits,
    total_amount, payment_status, payment_mode, notes, meal_session, delivery_charges
  )
  VALUES (
    p_customer_id, p_menu_item_id, p_order_type, p_plan_id, p_plan_credits,
    p_total_amount, p_payment_status, p_payment_mode, p_notes, p_meal_session, p_delivery_charges
  )
  RETURNING id INTO v_order_id;

  IF p_order_type = 'one_time' THEN
    INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
    VALUES (v_order_id, p_start_date, 'pending', v_credits_per_day);
  ELSE
    v_num_days := FLOOR(p_plan_credits::NUMERIC / v_credits_per_day);
    v_remainder := p_plan_credits - (v_num_days * v_credits_per_day);
    
    FOR v_i IN 0..(v_num_days - 1) LOOP
      INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
      VALUES (v_order_id, p_start_date + (v_i || ' days')::INTERVAL, 'pending', v_credits_per_day);
    END LOOP;
    
    IF v_remainder > 0 THEN
      INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
      VALUES (v_order_id, p_start_date + (v_num_days || ' days')::INTERVAL, 'pending', v_remainder);
    END IF;
  END IF;

  RETURN v_order_id;
END;
$$;

  c_reg_v UUID; c_reg_nv UUID; c_stud_v UUID; c_addon UUID;

  p3r UUID; p7r UUID; p30r UUID;
  p3s UUID; p7s UUID; p30s UUID;
  p7a UUID; p30a UUID;
BEGIN
  -- Deactivate old demo items (keeps your existing order history)
  UPDATE menu_items SET active = false WHERE active = true;
  UPDATE plans SET active = false WHERE active = true;
  DELETE FROM plan_menu_pricing;

  SELECT id INTO c_reg_nv FROM menu_categories WHERE name = 'Regular - Non-Veg';
  SELECT id INTO c_stud_v FROM menu_categories WHERE name = 'Student - Veg';

  INSERT INTO menu_items (category_id, name, price, cost, active) VALUES (c_reg_v, 'North Indian Pack', 145, 0, true) RETURNING id INTO i_rnv;
  INSERT INTO menu_items (category_id, name, price, cost, active) VALUES (c_reg_v, 'Protein Pack', 150, 0, true) RETURNING id INTO i_prv;
  INSERT INTO menu_items (category_id, name, price, cost, active) VALUES (c_reg_nv, 'South Indian Pack', 175, 0, true) RETURNING id INTO i_srn;
  INSERT INTO menu_items (category_id, name, price, cost, active) VALUES (c_reg_nv, 'North Indian Pack', 180, 0, true) RETURNING id INTO i_rnn;
  INSERT INTO menu_items (category_id, name, price, cost, active) VALUES (c_stud_v, 'South Indian Student Pack', 100, 0, true) RETURNING id INTO i_ssv;
  INSERT INTO menu_items (category_id, name, price, cost, active) VALUES (c_stud_v, 'North Indian Student Pack', 110, 0, true) RETURNING id INTO i_nsv;
  INSERT INTO menu_items (category_id, name, price, cost, active) VALUES (c_addon, 'Snacks (Add Ons)', 60, 0, true) RETURNING id INTO i_snack;

  -- Plans
  INSERT INTO plans (name, credits, duration_days, plan_type, bonus_credits, active) 
    SELECT '3-Day Regular', 3, 3, 'regular', 0, true WHERE NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM plans WHERE name = '3-Day Regular');
  INSERT INTO plans (name, credits, duration_days, plan_type, bonus_credits, active) 
    SELECT '7-Day Regular', 7, 7, 'regular', 0, true WHERE NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM plans WHERE name = '7-Day Regular');
  INSERT INTO plans (name, credits, duration_days, plan_type, bonus_credits, active) 
    SELECT '30-Day Regular (+1 Free)', 31, 30, 'regular', 1, true WHERE NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM plans WHERE name = '30-Day Regular (+1 Free)');
  INSERT INTO plans (name, credits, duration_days, plan_type, bonus_credits, active)

  INSERT INTO plans (name, credits, duration_days, plan_type, bonus_credits, active) 
    SELECT '7-Day Student', 7, 7, 'student', 0, true WHERE NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM plans WHERE name = '7-Day Student');

-- Temporarily remove old views.
-- They are recreated at the end of the full migration.
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS public.subscription_addon_overview;
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS public.subscription_delivery_timeline;
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS public.subscription_overview;

CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS "uuid-ossp";

-- customers
CREATE TABLE customers (
id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
name TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (char_length(trim(name)) > 0),
contact TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (char_length(trim(contact)) >= 7),
address TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (char_length(trim(address)) > 0),
created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

-- menu_categories
CREATE TABLE menu_categories (
id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
name TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE CHECK (char_length(trim(name)) > 0),
sort_order INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0
);

-- menu_items
CREATE TABLE menu_items (
id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
category_id UUID REFERENCES menu_categories(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
name TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (char_length(trim(name)) > 0),
price NUMERIC(10,2) NOT NULL CHECK (price >= 0),
cost NUMERIC(10,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 CHECK (cost >= 0),
active BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT true,
created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

-- plans
CREATE TABLE plans (
id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
name TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (char_length(trim(name)) > 0),
credits INTEGER NOT NULL CHECK (credits > 0),
active BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT true,
created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

INSERT INTO plans (name, credits) VALUES
('7-Meal Plan', 7),
('30-Meal Plan', 30);

-- orders
CREATE TABLE orders (
id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
customer_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES customers(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT,
menu_item_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES menu_items(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT,
order_type TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (order_type IN ('one_time', 'subscription')),
plan_id UUID REFERENCES plans(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT,
plan_credits INTEGER CHECK (plan_credits > 0),
credits_used INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
total_amount NUMERIC(10,2) NOT NULL CHECK (total_amount >= 0),
payment_status TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'not_paid'
CHECK (payment_status IN ('paid', 'not_paid')),
payment_mode TEXT CHECK (payment_mode IN (
'cash', 'upi', 'bank_transfer', 'card', 'other'
)),
notes TEXT,
created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
CONSTRAINT subscription_needs_plan CHECK (
(order_type = 'subscription' AND plan_id IS NOT NULL AND plan_credits IS NOT NULL)
OR
(order_type = 'one_time' AND plan_id IS NULL AND plan_credits IS NULL)
),
CONSTRAINT credits_used_within_plan CHECK (
plan_credits IS NULL OR credits_used <= plan_credits
)
);

-- deliveries
CREATE TABLE deliveries (
id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
order_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES orders(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
scheduled_date DATE NOT NULL,
status TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending'
CHECK (status IN ('pending', 'delivered', 'missed', 'cancelled')),
notes TEXT,
created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
UNIQUE (order_id, scheduled_date)
);

CREATE INDEX idx_deliveries_scheduled_date ON deliveries (scheduled_date);
CREATE INDEX idx_deliveries_order_id ON deliveries (order_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_deliveries_status ON deliveries (status);

-- trigger function
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION handle_delivery_status_change()
RETURNS TRIGGER
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
AS $$
DECLARE
v_order_type TEXT;
v_plan_credits INTEGER;
v_credits_used INTEGER;
v_latest_date DATE;
BEGIN
IF TG_OP = 'UPDATE' AND OLD.status = NEW.status THEN
RETURN NEW;
END IF;

SELECT order_type, plan_credits, credits_used
INTO v_order_type, v_plan_credits, v_credits_used
FROM orders
WHERE id = NEW.order_id;

-- on delivered: increment credits_used
IF NEW.status = 'delivered' AND OLD.status != 'delivered' THEN
UPDATE orders
SET credits_used = credits_used + 1
WHERE id = NEW.order_id;
END IF;

-- on missed: extend schedule for subscriptions only
IF NEW.status = 'missed' AND OLD.status != 'missed' THEN
IF v_order_type = 'subscription' THEN
SELECT credits_used INTO v_credits_used
FROM orders WHERE id = NEW.order_id;

text
  IF v_credits_used < v_plan_credits THEN
    SELECT MAX(scheduled_date)
      INTO v_latest_date
      FROM deliveries
     WHERE order_id = NEW.order_id;

    INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status)
      VALUES (NEW.order_id, v_latest_date + INTERVAL '1 day', 'pending')
      ON CONFLICT (order_id, scheduled_date) DO NOTHING;
  END IF;
END IF;
END IF;

RETURN NEW;
END;

CREATE TRIGGER trg_delivery_status_change
AFTER UPDATE OF status ON deliveries
FOR EACH ROW
EXECUTE FUNCTION handle_delivery_status_change();

-- RLS
ALTER TABLE customers ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE menu_categories ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE menu_items ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE plans ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE orders ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE deliveries ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

CREATE POLICY "allow_all_customers" ON customers FOR ALL USING (true) WITH CHECK (true);
CREATE POLICY "allow_all_menu_categories" ON menu_categories FOR ALL USING (true) WITH CHECK (true);
CREATE POLICY "allow_all_menu_items" ON menu_items FOR ALL USING (true) WITH CHECK (true);
CREATE POLICY "allow_all_plans" ON plans FOR ALL USING (true) WITH CHECK (true);
CREATE POLICY "allow_all_orders" ON orders FOR ALL USING (true) WITH CHECK (true);
CREATE POLICY "allow_all_deliveries" ON deliveries FOR ALL USING (true) WITH CHECK (true);

('Thali', 1),
('Salad', 2),
('Snacks', 3);

INSERT INTO menu_items (category_id, name, price, cost, active)
SELECT c.id, 'Veg Thali', 120.00, 55.00, true FROM menu_categories c WHERE c.name = 'Thali'
UNION ALL
SELECT c.id, 'Non-Veg Thali', 150.00, 75.00, true FROM menu_categories c WHERE c.name = 'Thali'
UNION ALL

-- ============================================================
-- CLEANUP: Remove conflicting views/tables (not yours)
-- ============================================================
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS subscription_overview CASCADE;
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS subscription_offers CASCADE;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS subscription_offers CASCADE;

DO $$
DECLARE
v RECORD;
BEGIN
FOR v IN SELECT viewname FROM pg_views WHERE schemaname = 'public' AND viewname LIKE 'subscription%' LOOP
EXECUTE 'DROP VIEW IF EXISTS public.' || quote_ident(v.viewname) || ' CASCADE';
END LOOP;
END $$;

-- ============================================================
-- UPGRADE: Add new columns safely
-- ============================================================
ALTER TABLE orders ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS meal_session TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'lunch'
CHECK (meal_session IN ('lunch', 'dinner', 'both'));

ALTER TABLE deliveries ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS credits_burn INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1 CHECK (credits_burn > 0);

ALTER TABLE plans ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS duration_days INTEGER;
ALTER TABLE plans ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS plan_type TEXT CHECK (plan_type IN ('regular', 'student', 'addon'));
ALTER TABLE plans ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS bonus_credits INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0;

ALTER TABLE orders ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS delivery_charges NUMERIC(10,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 CHECK (delivery_charges >= 0);

-- ============================================================
-- NEW TABLE: Pricing matrix
-- ============================================================
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS plan_menu_pricing (
id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
plan_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES plans(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
menu_item_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES menu_items(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
price NUMERIC(10,2) NOT NULL CHECK (price >= 0),
active BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT true,
created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
UNIQUE (plan_id, menu_item_id)
);

ALTER TABLE plan_menu_pricing ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
DROP POLICY IF EXISTS "allow_all_plan_menu_pricing" ON plan_menu_pricing;
CREATE POLICY "allow_all_plan_menu_pricing" ON plan_menu_pricing FOR ALL USING (true) WITH CHECK (true);

-- ============================================================
-- FUNCTIONS: Updated trigger + order creation
-- ============================================================
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION handle_delivery_status_change()
RETURNS TRIGGER
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
AS $$
DECLARE
v_order_type TEXT;
v_plan_credits INTEGER;
v_credits_used INTEGER;
v_latest_date DATE;
v_meal_session TEXT;
v_credits_burn INTEGER;
BEGIN
IF TG_OP = 'UPDATE' AND OLD.status = NEW.status THEN
RETURN NEW;
END IF;

SELECT order_type, plan_credits, credits_used, meal_session
INTO v_order_type, v_plan_credits, v_credits_used, v_meal_session
FROM orders WHERE id = NEW.order_id;

v_credits_burn := CASE WHEN v_meal_session = 'both' THEN 2 ELSE 1 END;

IF NEW.status = 'delivered' AND OLD.status != 'delivered' THEN
UPDATE orders
SET credits_used = LEAST(credits_used + v_credits_burn, plan_credits)
WHERE id = NEW.order_id;
END IF;

IF NEW.status = 'missed' AND OLD.status != 'missed' THEN
IF v_order_type = 'subscription' THEN
SELECT credits_used INTO v_credits_used FROM orders WHERE id = NEW.order_id;
IF v_credits_used < v_plan_credits THEN
SELECT MAX(scheduled_date) INTO v_latest_date FROM deliveries WHERE order_id = NEW.order_id;
INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
VALUES (NEW.order_id, v_latest_date + INTERVAL '1 day', 'pending', v_credits_burn)
ON CONFLICT (order_id, scheduled_date) DO NOTHING;
END IF;
END IF;
END IF;

RETURN NEW;
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION create_order_with_deliveries(
p_customer_id UUID,
p_menu_item_id UUID,
p_order_type TEXT,
p_plan_id UUID,
p_plan_credits INTEGER,
p_total_amount NUMERIC,
p_payment_status TEXT,
p_payment_mode TEXT,
p_notes TEXT,
p_start_date DATE,
p_meal_session TEXT DEFAULT 'lunch',
p_delivery_charges NUMERIC DEFAULT 0
)
RETURNS UUID
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public
AS $$
DECLARE
v_order_id UUID;
v_menu_active BOOLEAN;
v_credits_per_day INTEGER;
v_num_days INTEGER;
v_remainder INTEGER;
v_i INTEGER;
BEGIN
SELECT active INTO v_menu_active FROM menu_items WHERE id = p_menu_item_id;
IF v_menu_active IS NULL THEN RAISE EXCEPTION 'Menu item not found';
ELSIF v_menu_active = false THEN RAISE EXCEPTION 'This menu item is no longer active';
END IF;

IF p_order_type = 'subscription' AND (p_plan_id IS NULL OR p_plan_credits IS NULL) THEN
RAISE EXCEPTION 'Subscription orders require a plan';
END IF;
IF p_start_date IS NULL THEN RAISE EXCEPTION 'A delivery start date is required'; END IF;

v_credits_per_day := CASE WHEN p_meal_session = 'both' THEN 2 ELSE 1 END;

INSERT INTO orders (
customer_id, menu_item_id, order_type, plan_id, plan_credits,
total_amount, payment_status, payment_mode, notes, meal_session, delivery_charges
)
VALUES (
p_customer_id, p_menu_item_id, p_order_type, p_plan_id, p_plan_credits,
p_total_amount, p_payment_status, p_payment_mode, p_notes, p_meal_session, p_delivery_charges
)
RETURNING id INTO v_order_id;

IF p_order_type = 'one_time' THEN
INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
VALUES (v_order_id, p_start_date, 'pending', v_credits_per_day);
ELSE
v_num_days := FLOOR(p_plan_credits::NUMERIC / v_credits_per_day);
v_remainder := p_plan_credits - (v_num_days * v_credits_per_day);

text
FOR v_i IN 0..(v_num_days - 1) LOOP
  INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
  VALUES (v_order_id, p_start_date + (v_i || ' days')::INTERVAL, 'pending', v_credits_per_day);
END LOOP;

IF v_remainder > 0 THEN
  INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
  VALUES (v_order_id, p_start_date + (v_num_days || ' days')::INTERVAL, 'pending', v_remainder);
END IF;
END IF;

RETURN v_order_id;
END;

-- ============================================================
-- CLEANUP: Remove conflicting views/tables (not yours)
-- ============================================================
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS subscription_overview CASCADE;
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS subscription_offers CASCADE;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS subscription_offers CASCADE;

DO $$
DECLARE
    v RECORD;
BEGIN
    FOR v IN SELECT viewname FROM pg_views WHERE schemaname = 'public' AND viewname LIKE 'subscription%' LOOP
        EXECUTE 'DROP VIEW IF EXISTS public.' || quote_ident(v.viewname) || ' CASCADE';
    END LOOP;
END $$;

-- ============================================================
-- UPGRADE: Add new columns safely
-- ============================================================
ALTER TABLE orders ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS meal_session TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'lunch' 
  CHECK (meal_session IN ('lunch', 'dinner', 'both'));

ALTER TABLE deliveries ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS credits_burn INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1 CHECK (credits_burn > 0);

ALTER TABLE plans ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS duration_days INTEGER;
ALTER TABLE plans ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS plan_type TEXT CHECK (plan_type IN ('regular', 'student', 'addon'));
ALTER TABLE plans ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS bonus_credits INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0;

ALTER TABLE orders ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS delivery_charges NUMERIC(10,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 CHECK (delivery_charges >= 0);

-- ============================================================
-- NEW TABLE: Pricing matrix
-- ============================================================
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS plan_menu_pricing (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  plan_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES plans(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  menu_item_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES menu_items(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  price NUMERIC(10,2) NOT NULL CHECK (price >= 0),
  active BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT true,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  UNIQUE (plan_id, menu_item_id)
);

ALTER TABLE plan_menu_pricing ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
DROP POLICY IF EXISTS "allow_all_plan_menu_pricing" ON plan_menu_pricing;
CREATE POLICY "allow_all_plan_menu_pricing" ON plan_menu_pricing FOR ALL USING (true) WITH CHECK (true);

-- ============================================================
-- FUNCTIONS: Updated trigger + order creation
-- ============================================================
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION handle_delivery_status_change()
RETURNS TRIGGER
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_order_type    TEXT;
  v_plan_credits  INTEGER;
  v_credits_used  INTEGER;
  v_latest_date   DATE;
  v_meal_session  TEXT;
  v_credits_burn  INTEGER;
BEGIN
  IF TG_OP = 'UPDATE' AND OLD.status = NEW.status THEN
    RETURN NEW;
  END IF;

  SELECT order_type, plan_credits, credits_used, meal_session
    INTO v_order_type, v_plan_credits, v_credits_used, v_meal_session
    FROM orders WHERE id = NEW.order_id;
  
  v_credits_burn := CASE WHEN v_meal_session = 'both' THEN 2 ELSE 1 END;

  IF NEW.status = 'delivered' AND OLD.status != 'delivered' THEN
    UPDATE orders
       SET credits_used = LEAST(credits_used + v_credits_burn, plan_credits)
     WHERE id = NEW.order_id;
  END IF;

  IF NEW.status = 'missed' AND OLD.status != 'missed' THEN
    IF v_order_type = 'subscription' THEN
      SELECT credits_used INTO v_credits_used FROM orders WHERE id = NEW.order_id;
      IF v_credits_used < v_plan_credits THEN
        SELECT MAX(scheduled_date) INTO v_latest_date FROM deliveries WHERE order_id = NEW.order_id;
        INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
          VALUES (NEW.order_id, v_latest_date + INTERVAL '1 day', 'pending', v_credits_burn)
          ON CONFLICT (order_id, scheduled_date) DO NOTHING;
      END IF;
    END IF;
  END IF;

  RETURN NEW;
END;
$$;

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION create_order_with_deliveries(
  p_customer_id    UUID,
  p_menu_item_id   UUID,
  p_order_type     TEXT,
  p_plan_id        UUID,
  p_plan_credits   INTEGER,
  p_total_amount   NUMERIC,
  p_payment_status TEXT,
  p_payment_mode   TEXT,
  p_notes          TEXT,
  p_start_date     DATE,
  p_meal_session   TEXT DEFAULT 'lunch',
  p_delivery_charges NUMERIC DEFAULT 0
)
RETURNS UUID
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_order_id    UUID;
  v_menu_active BOOLEAN;
  v_credits_per_day INTEGER;
  v_num_days    INTEGER;
  v_remainder   INTEGER;
  v_i           INTEGER;
BEGIN
  SELECT active INTO v_menu_active FROM menu_items WHERE id = p_menu_item_id;
  IF v_menu_active IS NULL THEN RAISE EXCEPTION 'Menu item not found';
  ELSIF v_menu_active = false THEN RAISE EXCEPTION 'This menu item is no longer active';
  END IF;

  IF p_order_type = 'subscription' AND (p_plan_id IS NULL OR p_plan_credits IS NULL) THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Subscription orders require a plan';
  END IF;
  IF p_start_date IS NULL THEN RAISE EXCEPTION 'A delivery start date is required'; END IF;

  v_credits_per_day := CASE WHEN p_meal_session = 'both' THEN 2 ELSE 1 END;

  INSERT INTO orders (
    customer_id, menu_item_id, order_type, plan_id, plan_credits,
    total_amount, payment_status, payment_mode, notes, meal_session, delivery_charges
  )
  VALUES (
    p_customer_id, p_menu_item_id, p_order_type, p_plan_id, p_plan_credits,
    p_total_amount, p_payment_status, p_payment_mode, p_notes, p_meal_session, p_delivery_charges
  )
  RETURNING id INTO v_order_id;

  IF p_order_type = 'one_time' THEN
    INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
    VALUES (v_order_id, p_start_date, 'pending', v_credits_per_day);
  ELSE
    v_num_days := FLOOR(p_plan_credits::NUMERIC / v_credits_per_day);
    v_remainder := p_plan_credits - (v_num_days * v_credits_per_day);
    
    FOR v_i IN 0..(v_num_days - 1) LOOP
      INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
      VALUES (v_order_id, p_start_date + (v_i || ' days')::INTERVAL, 'pending', v_credits_per_day);
    END LOOP;
    
    IF v_remainder > 0 THEN
      INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
      VALUES (v_order_id, p_start_date + (v_num_days || ' days')::INTERVAL, 'pending', v_remainder);

  END IF;

END;

SQL
-- ============================================================
-- SCHEMA UPGRADE: Real Menu + Pricing Matrix + Meal Session
-- ============================================================

-- 1. Add columns safely
ALTER TABLE orders ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS meal_session TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'lunch' 
  CHECK (meal_session IN ('lunch', 'dinner', 'both'));

ALTER TABLE deliveries ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS credits_burn INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1 CHECK (credits_burn > 0);

ALTER TABLE plans ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS duration_days INTEGER;
ALTER TABLE plans ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS plan_type TEXT CHECK (plan_type IN ('regular', 'student', 'addon'));
ALTER TABLE plans ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS bonus_credits INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0;

ALTER TABLE orders ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS delivery_charges NUMERIC(10,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 CHECK (delivery_charges >= 0);

-- 2. Create pricing matrix
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS plan_menu_pricing (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  plan_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES plans(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  menu_item_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES menu_items(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  price NUMERIC(10,2) NOT NULL CHECK (price >= 0),
  active BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT true,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  UNIQUE (plan_id, menu_item_id)
);

ALTER TABLE plan_menu_pricing ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
DROP POLICY IF EXISTS "allow_all_plan_menu_pricing" ON plan_menu_pricing;
CREATE POLICY "allow_all_plan_menu_pricing" ON plan_menu_pricing FOR ALL USING (true) WITH CHECK (true);

-- 3. Update trigger function
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION handle_delivery_status_change()
RETURNS TRIGGER
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_order_type    TEXT;
  v_plan_credits  INTEGER;
  v_credits_used  INTEGER;
  v_latest_date   DATE;
  v_meal_session  TEXT;
  v_credits_burn  INTEGER;
BEGIN
  IF TG_OP = 'UPDATE' AND OLD.status = NEW.status THEN
    RETURN NEW;
  END IF;

  SELECT order_type, plan_credits, credits_used, meal_session
    INTO v_order_type, v_plan_credits, v_credits_used, v_meal_session
    FROM orders WHERE id = NEW.order_id;
  
  v_credits_burn := CASE WHEN v_meal_session = 'both' THEN 2 ELSE 1 END;

  IF NEW.status = 'delivered' AND OLD.status != 'delivered' THEN
    UPDATE orders
       SET credits_used = LEAST(credits_used + v_credits_burn, plan_credits)
     WHERE id = NEW.order_id;
  END IF;

  IF NEW.status = 'missed' AND OLD.status != 'missed' THEN
    IF v_order_type = 'subscription' THEN
      SELECT credits_used INTO v_credits_used FROM orders WHERE id = NEW.order_id;
      IF v_credits_used < v_plan_credits THEN
        SELECT MAX(scheduled_date) INTO v_latest_date FROM deliveries WHERE order_id = NEW.order_id;
        INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
          VALUES (NEW.order_id, v_latest_date + INTERVAL '1 day', 'pending', v_credits_burn)
          ON CONFLICT (order_id, scheduled_date) DO NOTHING;
      END IF;
    END IF;
  END IF;

  RETURN NEW;
END;
$$;

-- 4. Update order creation function
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION create_order_with_deliveries(
  p_customer_id    UUID,
  p_menu_item_id   UUID,
  p_order_type     TEXT,
  p_plan_id        UUID,
  p_plan_credits   INTEGER,
  p_total_amount   NUMERIC,
  p_payment_status TEXT,
  p_payment_mode   TEXT,
  p_notes          TEXT,
  p_start_date     DATE,
  p_meal_session   TEXT DEFAULT 'lunch',
  p_delivery_charges NUMERIC DEFAULT 0
)
RETURNS UUID
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_order_id    UUID;
  v_menu_active BOOLEAN;
  v_credits_per_day INTEGER;
  v_num_days    INTEGER;
  v_remainder   INTEGER;
  v_i           INTEGER;
BEGIN
  SELECT active INTO v_menu_active FROM menu_items WHERE id = p_menu_item_id;
  IF v_menu_active IS NULL THEN RAISE EXCEPTION 'Menu item not found';
  ELSIF v_menu_active = false THEN RAISE EXCEPTION 'This menu item is no longer active';
  END IF;

  IF p_order_type = 'subscription' AND (p_plan_id IS NULL OR p_plan_credits IS NULL) THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Subscription orders require a plan';
  END IF;
  IF p_start_date IS NULL THEN RAISE EXCEPTION 'A delivery start date is required'; END IF;

  v_credits_per_day := CASE WHEN p_meal_session = 'both' THEN 2 ELSE 1 END;

  INSERT INTO orders (
    customer_id, menu_item_id, order_type, plan_id, plan_credits,
    total_amount, payment_status, payment_mode, notes, meal_session, delivery_charges
  )
  VALUES (
    p_customer_id, p_menu_item_id, p_order_type, p_plan_id, p_plan_credits,
    p_total_amount, p_payment_status, p_payment_mode, p_notes, p_meal_session, p_delivery_charges
  )
  RETURNING id INTO v_order_id;

  IF p_order_type = 'one_time' THEN
    INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
    VALUES (v_order_id, p_start_date, 'pending', v_credits_per_day);
  ELSE
    v_num_days := FLOOR(p_plan_credits::NUMERIC / v_credits_per_day);
    v_remainder := p_plan_credits - (v_num_days * v_credits_per_day);
    
    FOR v_i IN 0..(v_num_days - 1) LOOP
      INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
      VALUES (v_order_id, p_start_date + (v_i || ' days')::INTERVAL, 'pending', v_credits_per_day);
    END LOOP;
    
    IF v_remainder > 0 THEN
      INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
      VALUES (v_order_id, p_start_date + (v_num_days || ' days')::INTERVAL, 'pending', v_remainder);
    END IF;
  END IF;

  RETURN v_order_id;
END;
$$;

FROM public.subscription_offers so
JOIN public.pricing_groups pg ON pg.id = so.pricing_group_id
JOIN public.menu_items mi ON mi.id = so.menu_item_id
JOIN public.plans p ON p.id = so.plan_id
ORDER BY pg.name, mi.name, p.duration_days, so.offer_kind;
Then you should see approximately 25 offer rows, including things such as:

text
regular_veg_south_7
regular_nonveg_north_30
student_veg_south_30
student_snack_addon_7
student_snack_standalone_30

kimi-k2.6
Quick Fix — Drop the Conflicting View First
Supabase (or a previous experiment) created a view called subscription_overview that references old column names. It's blocking our schema changes.

Run this ONE line first in your SQL Editor:

SQL
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS subscription_overview;
Then re-run the exact same SQL block I gave you in the previous message (the big schema upgrade with plan_menu_pricing, meal_session, delivery_charges, etc.).

Why This Happened
A view is like a saved query that reads from your tables. If it references a column you're trying to change, Postgres blocks the change. The view subscription_overview references a column called unit_price which doesn't exist in our schema — it was likely auto-generated by Supabase AI or left over from an earlier test. We don't need it.

After It Works
Tell me: "SQL ran successfully, view dropped" and I'll confirm the next step (running scriptF.ps1).

gpt-5.6-terra-xhigh
This is a normal migration-order error, not a data-loss problem.

subscription_overview currently uses deliveries.unit_price, so PostgreSQL will not let us change that column’s numeric type while the view exists.

Because the catalog SQL was wrapped in:

SQL
BEGIN;
...
COMMIT;
the failed migration was rolled back. Your existing customers, orders, deliveries, and current views are still safe.

Fix
In the large Catalog SQL script I gave you, find the very top:

SQL
BEGIN;

CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS "uuid-ossp";
Replace it with this:

SQL
BEGIN;

-- Temporarily remove old read-only views.
-- They are recreated near the end of the same migration.
-- No customer/order/delivery data is deleted.
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS public.subscription_addon_overview;
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS public.subscription_delivery_timeline;
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS public.subscription_overview;

CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS "uuid-ossp";
Then run the entire Catalog SQL script again, from the new BEGIN; at the top all the way through its final:

SQL
COMMIT;
Why this is safe
These are database views, not tables:

text
subscription_overview
subscription_delivery_timeline
subscription_addon_overview
They contain no stored customer/order/delivery data. They are saved query definitions used by the Lunchmate frontend.

The migration will:

Temporarily remove the old views.
Upgrade unit_price precision.
Add the menu catalog, package offers, delivery calculation, Student verification, Lunch/Dinner logic, etc.
Create the updated views again before committing.
Your app may show an error for a few seconds if it is open during the migration. Just refresh it after SQL succeeds.

Do not do this
Do not use:

SQL
DROP VIEW ... CASCADE;
The plain DROP VIEW IF EXISTS commands above are enough and safer.

# Script F - Final NewOrder.jsx with student lunch-only lock + delivery charges

@'
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { supabase } from '../lib/supabase'
import { todayDateString, addDaysToDateString } from '../lib/date'
import CustomerPicker from '../components/CustomerPicker'
import Alert from '../components/Alert'

const PAYMENT_MODES = [
  { value: 'cash', label: 'Cash' },
  { value: 'upi', label: 'UPI' },
  { value: 'bank_transfer', label: 'Bank Transfer' },
  { value: 'card', label: 'Card' },
  { value: 'other', label: 'Other' },
]

function getPlanTypeFromCategory(catName) {
  if (!catName) return 'regular'
  const lower = catName.toLowerCase()
  if (lower.includes('student')) return 'student'
  if (lower.includes('addon') || lower.includes('add-on')) return 'addon'
  return 'regular'
}

function calculateDeliveryCharge(distanceKm) {
  const d = Number(distanceKm)
  if (isNaN(d) || d <= 0) return 0
  if (d <= 1.0) return 5.0
  const extra = d - 1.0
  const fullKm = Math.floor(extra)
  const remainderM = (extra - fullKm) * 1000
  const hundreds = Math.ceil(remainderM / 100)
  return 5.0 + (fullKm * 4.0) + (hundreds * 0.30)
}

export default function NewOrder() {
  const [customer, setCustomer] = useState(null)
  const [orderType, setOrderType] = useState('subscription')
  const [categories, setCategories] = useState([])
  const [items, setItems] = useState([])
  const [selectedCategory, setSelectedCategory] = useState('')
  const [selectedItem, setSelectedItem] = useState(null)
  const [plans, setPlans] = useState([])
  const [selectedPlan, setSelectedPlan] = useState(null)
  const [planPrice, setPlanPrice] = useState(0)
  const [mealSession, setMealSession] = useState('lunch')
  const [startDate, setStartDate] = useState(addDaysToDateString(todayDateString(), 1))
  const [distanceKm, setDistanceKm] = useState('')
  const [deliveryChargePerDay, setDeliveryChargePerDay] = useState(0)
  const [paymentStatus, setPaymentStatus] = useState('not_paid')
  const [paymentMode, setPaymentMode] = useState('cash')
  const [notes, setNotes] = useState('')
  const [submitting, setSubmitting] = useState(false)
  const [error, setError] = useState('')
  const [success, setSuccess] = useState('')

  useEffect(() => {
    async function load() {
      const [catRes, itemRes] = await Promise.all([
        supabase.from('menu_categories').select('id, name, sort_order').order('sort_order'),
        supabase.from('menu_items').select('id, name, price, category_id').eq('active', true).order('name'),
      ])
      if (!catRes.error) setCategories(catRes.data || [])
      if (!itemRes.error) setItems(itemRes.data || [])
    }
    load()
  }, [])

  const filteredItems = selectedCategory ? items.filter(i => i.category_id === selectedCategory) : []
  const selectedCatObj = categories.find(c => c.id === selectedCategory)
  const planType = getPlanTypeFromCategory(selectedCatObj?.name)
  const isStudent = planType === 'student'
  const isAddon = planType === 'addon'
  const isRegular = planType === 'regular'

  useEffect(() => {
    if (isStudent || isAddon) setMealSession('lunch')
  }, [isStudent, isAddon])

  useEffect(() => {
    async function loadPlans() {
      if (!selectedItem) {
        setPlans([])
        setSelectedPlan(null)
        setPlanPrice(0)
        return
      }
      const { data, error } = await supabase
        .from('plans')
        .select('id, name, credits, duration_days, bonus_credits')
        .eq('active', true)
        .eq('plan_type', planType)
        .order('credits')
      
      if (!error) setPlans(data || [])
      setSelectedPlan(null)
      setPlanPrice(0)
    }
    loadPlans()
  }, [selectedItem, planType])

  useEffect(() => {
    async function loadPrice() {
      if (!selectedItem || !selectedPlan || orderType !== 'subscription') {
        setPlanPrice(0)
        return
      }
      const { data, error } = await supabase
        .from('plan_menu_pricing')
        .select('price')
        .eq('plan_id', selectedPlan.id)
        .eq('menu_item_id', selectedItem.id)
        .eq('active', true)
        .single()
      
      if (!error && data) setPlanPrice(Number(data.price))
      else setPlanPrice(0)
    }
    loadPrice()
  }, [selectedItem, selectedPlan, orderType])

  useEffect(() => {
    const charge = calculateDeliveryCharge(distanceKm)
    setDeliveryChargePerDay(charge)
  }, [distanceKm])

  const creditsPerDay = mealSession === 'both' ? 2 : 1
  const numDays = selectedPlan ? Math.floor(selectedPlan.credits / creditsPerDay) : 0
  const remainder = selectedPlan ? selectedPlan.credits - (numDays * creditsPerDay) : 0
  const totalDeliveryDays = orderType === 'subscription' && selectedPlan ? numDays + (remainder > 0 ? 1 : 0) : 1
  const totalDeliveryCharges = deliveryChargePerDay * totalDeliveryDays

  const baseAmount = orderType === 'subscription' ? planPrice : (selectedItem ? Number(selectedItem.price) : 0)
  const totalAmount = baseAmount + totalDeliveryCharges

  function resetForm() {
    setCustomer(null)
    setOrderType('subscription')
    setSelectedCategory('')
    setSelectedItem(null)
    setSelectedPlan(null)
    setPlanPrice(0)
    setMealSession('lunch')
    setStartDate(addDaysToDateString(todayDateString(), 1))
    setDistanceKm('')
    setDeliveryChargePerDay(0)
    setPaymentStatus('not_paid')
    setPaymentMode('cash')
    setNotes('')
  }

  function validate() {
    if (!customer) return 'Please select or create a customer.'
    if (!selectedItem) return 'Please select a menu item.'
    if (orderType === 'subscription' && !selectedPlan) return 'Please select a plan.'
    if (orderType === 'subscription' && planPrice <= 0) return 'Price not found for this plan+item. Check Supabase plan_menu_pricing table.'
    if (!startDate) return 'Please pick a delivery date.'
    if (startDate < todayDateString()) return 'Delivery date cannot be in the past.'
    if (totalAmount < 0) return 'Total amount cannot be negative.'
    return ''
  }

  async function handleSubmit(e) {
    e.preventDefault()
    setError('')
    setSuccess('')
    const validationError = validate()
    if (validationError) {
      setError(validationError)
      return
    }

    setSubmitting(true)
    const { error } = await supabase.rpc('create_order_with_deliveries', {
      p_customer_id: customer.id,
      p_menu_item_id: selectedItem.id,
      p_order_type: orderType,
      p_plan_id: orderType === 'subscription' ? selectedPlan.id : null,
      p_plan_credits: orderType === 'subscription' ? selectedPlan.credits : null,
      p_total_amount: totalAmount,
      p_payment_status: paymentStatus,
      p_payment_mode: paymentMode,
      p_notes: notes.trim() || null,
      p_start_date: startDate,
      p_meal_session: mealSession,
      p_delivery_charges: totalDeliveryCharges,
    })
    setSubmitting(false)

    if (error) {
      setError(`Failed to log order: ${error.message}`)
      return
    }

    const planDesc = orderType === 'subscription' 
      ? `${selectedPlan.credits} deliveries over ${totalDeliveryDays} days` 
      : '1 delivery'
    setSuccess(`Order logged! ${planDesc} scheduled starting ${startDate}.`)
    resetForm()
  }

  return (
    <div className="max-w-xl mx-auto bg-white rounded-lg shadow-sm border p-6">
      <h1 className="text-xl font-bold mb-4">New Order</h1>

      <Alert type="error" message={error} onClose={() => setError('')} />
      <Alert type="success" message={success} onClose={() => setSuccess('')} />

      <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-5">
        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Customer</label>
          <CustomerPicker selectedCustomer={customer} onSelect={setCustomer} />
        </div>

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Order Type</label>
          <div className="flex gap-4">
            <label className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
              <input
                type="radio"
                checked={orderType === 'subscription'}
                onChange={() => setOrderType('subscription')}
              />
              Subscription
            </label>
            <label className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
              <input
                type="radio"
                checked={orderType === 'one_time'}
                onChange={() => setOrderType('one_time')}
              />
              One-time
            </label>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Category</label>
          <select
            value={selectedCategory}
            onChange={(e) => { setSelectedCategory(e.target.value); setSelectedItem(null); setSelectedPlan(null); setPlanPrice(0); setMealSession('lunch') }}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
          >
            <option value="">Select category...</option>
            {categories.map((c) => (
              <option key={c.id} value={c.id}>{c.name}</option>
            ))}
          </select>
        </div>

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Menu Item</label>
          <select
            value={selectedItem?.id || ''}
            onChange={(e) => {
              const item = filteredItems.find(i => i.id === e.target.value)
              setSelectedItem(item || null)
            }}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
            disabled={!selectedCategory}
          >
            <option value="">Select item...</option>
            {filteredItems.map((i) => (
              <option key={i.id} value={i.id}>{i.name}</option>
            ))}
          </select>
        </div>

        {orderType === 'subscription' && selectedItem && (
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Plan</label>
            {plans.length === 0 ? (
              <p className="text-sm text-amber-600">No active plans for this category.</p>
            ) : (
              <select
                value={selectedPlan?.id || ''}
                onChange={(e) => {
                  const plan = plans.find(p => p.id === e.target.value)
                  setSelectedPlan(plan || null)
                }}
                className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
              >
                <option value="">Select plan...</option>
                {plans.map((p) => (
                  <option key={p.id} value={p.id}>
                    {p.name} ({p.credits} credits{p.bonus_credits > 0 ? ` incl. ${p.bonus_credits} free` : ''})
                  </option>
                ))}
              </select>
            )}
            {planPrice > 0 && (
              <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">Plan price: Rs.{planPrice.toFixed(2)}</p>
            )}
          </div>
        )}

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Meal Session</label>
          <div className="flex gap-4">
            {['lunch', 'dinner', 'both'].map((s) => (
              <label key={s} className={`flex items-center gap-2 text-sm capitalize ${(isStudent || isAddon) && s !== 'lunch' ? 'text-gray-400' : ''}`}>
                <input
                  type="radio"
                  checked={mealSession === s}
                  onChange={() => setMealSession(s)}
                  disabled={isStudent || isAddon}
                  readOnly={isStudent || isAddon}
                />
                {s}
              </label>
            ))}
          </div>
          {isStudent && <p className="text-xs text-amber-600 mt-1">Student plans are lunch only</p>}
          {isAddon && <p className="text-xs text-amber-600 mt-1">Add-ons are lunch only</p>}
          {isRegular && mealSession === 'both' && orderType === 'subscription' && (
            <p className="text-xs text-amber-600 mt-1">Burns 2 credits per day. Fewer total delivery days.</p>
          )}
        </div>

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">
            {orderType === 'subscription' ? 'Delivery Start Date' : 'Delivery Date'}
          </label>
          <input
            type="date"
            value={startDate}
            min={todayDateString()}
            onChange={(e) => setStartDate(e.target.value)}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
          />
        </div>

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Delivery Distance (km)</label>
          <input
            type="number"
            min="0"
            step="0.1"
            value={distanceKm}
            onChange={(e) => setDistanceKm(e.target.value)}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
            placeholder="e.g. 1.5"
          />
          {deliveryChargePerDay > 0 && (
            <div className="mt-1 text-xs text-gray-500 space-y-0.5">
              <p>Per day: Rs.{deliveryChargePerDay.toFixed(2)}</p>
              {orderType === 'subscription' && selectedPlan && (
                <p>{totalDeliveryDays} days x Rs.{deliveryChargePerDay.toFixed(2)} = Rs.{totalDeliveryCharges.toFixed(2)}</p>
              )}
              {orderType === 'one_time' && (
                <p>One-time: Rs.{totalDeliveryCharges.toFixed(2)}</p>
              )}
            </div>
          )}
        </div>

        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Payment Status</label>
            <select
              value={paymentStatus}
              onChange={(e) => setPaymentStatus(e.target.value)}
              className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
            >
              <option value="not_paid">Not Paid</option>
              <option value="paid">Paid</option>
            </select>
          </div>
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Payment Mode</label>
            <select
              value={paymentMode}
              onChange={(e) => setPaymentMode(e.target.value)}
              className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
            >
              {PAYMENT_MODES.map((m) => (
                <option key={m.value} value={m.value}>{m.label}</option>
              ))}
            </select>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Notes (optional)</label>
          <textarea
            value={notes}
            onChange={(e) => setNotes(e.target.value)}
            rows={2}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
            placeholder="Allergies, gate code, delivery instructions..."
          />
        </div>

        <div className="border-t pt-4 flex items-center justify-between">
          <div>
            <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Total Amount</p>
            <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-green-700">Rs.{totalAmount.toFixed(2)}</p>
            <p className="text-xs text-gray-400">
              {orderType === 'subscription' ? `Plan: Rs.${planPrice.toFixed(2)}` : `Item: Rs.${baseAmount.toFixed(2)}`} + Delivery: Rs.{totalDeliveryCharges.toFixed(2)}
            </p>
          </div>
          <button
            type="submit"
            disabled={submitting}
            className="bg-green-600 text-white px-5 py-2.5 rounded-md font-medium disabled:opacity-50"
          >
            {submitting ? 'Logging Order...' : 'Log Order'}
          </button>
        </div>
      </form>
    </div>
  )
}

Message from kimi-k2.6
gpt-5.6-terra-xhigh
Perfect. I have the final operating rules.

Final rules being implemented
Regular delivery fee

Up to 1.0 km = ₹5
After that: ₹4 per completed extra km
Remaining distance rounds up to next 100 m = ₹0.30 per 100 m
Examples match your values: 2.3 km = ₹9.90, 3.0 km = ₹13.00
Regular subscriptions

Customer pays upfront:
text
Pack food price + (delivery fee × included credits)
31-credit plans pay 31 delivery charges upfront.
Student subscriptions

Require verified Student ID / authorized verification.
Vegetarian only for now.
Lunch-only.
Main Student meal + attached snack add-on has free delivery.
Standalone Student Snack subscription has normal distance delivery charges.
Lunch/Dinner

Regular customers can use Lunch or Dinner.
Student customers cannot move Lunch to Dinner.
If a regular customer changes today’s Lunch to Dinner, it uses the same credit.
If they request an extra Dinner while their Lunch plan continues:
Extra Dinner becomes an additional due meal.
If they later miss a Lunch delivery, that missed Lunch settles the oldest delivered extra Dinner.
No replacement Lunch delivery is added in that case.
30-credit / 31-credit switching

Not allowed.
A 30-credit Protein Pack cannot be changed into a 31-credit pack.
Regular/Student offers cannot be switched between each other.
One-time orders

Remain available as a special/manual request at the bottom of Order Entry.
No normal public one-time menu prices will be seeded.
You manually enter approved food price for VIP/requested customers.
Run This Supabase SQL Upgrade
Open:

text
https://supabase.com/dashboard/project/ukrztdeqzbbroowcphwk/sql/new
Paste the full SQL below and click Run.

This is a schema/catalog upgrade. It preserves your existing test customers, orders, subscriptions, and deliveries.

SQL
BEGIN;

CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS "uuid-ossp";

-- ============================================================
-- 1. PLAN TERMS
-- Existing plans remain. Adds a 3-meal plan and duration metadata.
-- ============================================================

ALTER TABLE public.plans
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS plan_code TEXT,
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS duration_days INTEGER,
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS description TEXT;

CREATE UNIQUE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS plans_plan_code_unique
  ON public.plans (plan_code)
  WHERE plan_code IS NOT NULL;

UPDATE public.plans
SET duration_days = credits
WHERE duration_days IS NULL;

-- Attach stable codes to existing 7 and 30 meal plans.
UPDATE public.plans p
SET plan_code = 'plan_7',
    duration_days = 7
WHERE p.id = (
  SELECT id
  FROM public.plans
  WHERE plan_code IS NULL
    AND credits = 7
  ORDER BY created_at
  LIMIT 1
)
AND NOT EXISTS (
  SELECT 1 FROM public.plans WHERE plan_code = 'plan_7'
);

UPDATE public.plans p
SET plan_code = 'plan_30',
    duration_days = 30
WHERE p.id = (
  SELECT id
  FROM public.plans
  WHERE plan_code IS NULL
    AND credits = 30
  ORDER BY created_at
  LIMIT 1
)
AND NOT EXISTS (
  SELECT 1 FROM public.plans WHERE plan_code = 'plan_30'
);

INSERT INTO public.plans (
  plan_code,
  name,
  credits,
  duration_days,
  active,
  description
)
SELECT
  'plan_3',
  '3-Meal Plan',
  3,
  3,
  true,
  '3 successful meal credits'
WHERE NOT EXISTS (
  SELECT 1 FROM public.plans WHERE plan_code = 'plan_3'
);

-- ============================================================
-- 2. CUSTOMER STUDENT VERIFICATION
-- ============================================================

ALTER TABLE public.customers
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS student_verification_status TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'not_required',
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS student_id_number TEXT,
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS student_institution TEXT,
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS student_verified_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS student_verification_notes TEXT;

DO $$
BEGIN
  IF NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM pg_constraint
    WHERE conname = 'customers_student_verification_status_check'
  ) THEN
    ALTER TABLE public.customers
      ADD CONSTRAINT customers_student_verification_status_check
      CHECK (
        student_verification_status IN (
          'not_required',
          'pending',
          'verified',
          'rejected'
        )
      );
  END IF;
END;
$$;

-- ============================================================
-- 3. PRICING GROUPS
-- ============================================================

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS public.pricing_groups (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  code TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
  name TEXT NOT NULL,
  requires_student_verification BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT false,
  description TEXT,
  active BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT true,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

  WHERE catalog_code IS NOT NULL;

BEGIN
  IF NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM pg_constraint
    WHERE conname = 'menu_items_item_kind_check'
  ) THEN
    ALTER TABLE public.menu_items
      ADD CONSTRAINT menu_items_item_kind_check
      CHECK (item_kind IN ('meal_pack', 'snack'));
  END IF;
END;
$$;

-- ============================================================
-- 5. EDITABLE PACKAGE OFFERS
-- Every package price and included-credit rule lives here.
-- ============================================================

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS public.subscription_offers (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),

  offer_code TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
  pricing_group_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES public.pricing_groups(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT,
  menu_item_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES public.menu_items(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT,
  plan_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES public.plans(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT,

  offer_kind TEXT NOT NULL,
  package_price NUMERIC(12,2) NOT NULL CHECK (package_price >= 0),
  included_credits INTEGER NOT NULL CHECK (included_credits > 0),

  delivery_fee_policy TEXT NOT NULL,
  allow_lunch BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT true,
  allow_dinner BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT false,

  requires_parent_subscription BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT false,
  active BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT true,

  description TEXT,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

DO $$
BEGIN
  IF NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 FROM pg_constraint
    WHERE conname = 'subscription_offers_offer_kind_check'
  ) THEN
    ALTER TABLE public.subscription_offers
      ADD CONSTRAINT subscription_offers_offer_kind_check
      CHECK (
        offer_kind IN (
          'main_meal',
          'snack_addon',
          'standalone_snack'
        )
      );
  END IF;

  IF NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 FROM pg_constraint
    WHERE conname = 'subscription_offers_delivery_fee_policy_check'
  ) THEN
    ALTER TABLE public.subscription_offers
      ADD CONSTRAINT subscription_offers_delivery_fee_policy_check
      CHECK (delivery_fee_policy IN ('distance', 'included'));
  END IF;
END;
$$;

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS subscription_offers_group_idx
  ON public.subscription_offers(pricing_group_id);

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS subscription_offers_menu_idx
  ON public.subscription_offers(menu_item_id);

-- Seed actual Lunchmate offers from your flyers.
